  "content": "# Investigation Report\n\n## Summary\n\nThe change (commit `2e534d6da10`) modifies `GatherPools()` in all three allocator tiers (stable, incubating, experimental) to compute pool completeness _before_ filtering slices by node affinity, which allows `AllocationMode: All` to succeed for multi-node resource pools where only a subset of the pool's slices target the scheduling node. Previously, such pools were incorrectly marked as incomplete (because the per-node slice count did not match `ResourceSliceCount`), causing allocation to fail with \"pool is currently being updated.\"\n\n## Root Cause\n\nThe scope of the change is narrow in terms of files touched (4 files, `pools_{stable,incubating,experimental}.go` + test), but the behavioral impact is broad: any workload using `AllocationMode: All` with resource pools whose slices span multiple nodes will now successfully allocate, whereas before it was silently blocked. The core bug was in the `IsIncomplete` computation inside `GatherPools()` \u2014 it compared `len(pool.Slices)` (post-node-filter) against `pool.Slices[0].Spec.Pool.ResourceSliceCount` (the total across all nodes), which always mismatch for multi-node pools. The fix introduces a pre-filter completeness check using the full set of slices grouped by pool identifier.\n\n### Components affected:\n1. **Structured allocator pool gathering** \u2014 the `GatherPools()` function is the direct change site.\n2. **Scheduler DRA plugin Filter path** \u2014 `GatherPools()` is called from `Allocator.Allocate()` which is invoked during the `Filter` extension point, the scheduler's hot path evaluated for every node.\n3. **Downstream kubelet/device-plugin behavior** \u2014 the kubelet sees different `AllocationResult` contents (potentially more devices from a single pool), but the kubelet code itself is not changed and processes allocation results generically.\n\n## Evidence\n\n### The Commit Diff (2e534d6da10)\n\n**Files changed:**\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/stable/pools_stable.go` (lines 48-95, 140)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/incubating/pools_incubating.go` (lines 48-95, 140)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/experimental/pools_experimental.go` (lines 48-95, 162)\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/allocatortesting/allocator_testing.go` (lines 5093-5126)\n\n**Key change in `pools_stable.go`** (identical pattern in incubating/experimental):\n\nBefore (line ~99 of old code):\n```go\npool.IsIncomplete = int64(len(pool.Slices)) != pool.Slices[0].Spec.Pool.ResourceSliceCount\n```\n\nAfter (lines 58-95 new code):\n```go\n// Pre-filter: group ALL slices by pool, check completeness against total slice count and generation\nslicesByPool := make(map[poolIdentifier][]*resourceapi.ResourceSlice)\n// ... grouping logic ...\nincompletePools := sets.New[poolIdentifier]()\n// ... completeness check using full (unfiltered) slice set ...\n\n// Then later at line 143:\npool.IsIncomplete = incompletePools.Has(poolIdentifier{driver: pool.Driver.String(), pool: pool.Pool.String()})\n```\n\n### Allocation Logic That Depends on `IsIncomplete`\n\n**`allocator_stable.go:402-417`** \u2014 The `AllocationMode: All` handler iterates all pools and **rejects** the entire allocation if any pool is incomplete:\n```go\ncase resourceapi.DeviceAllocationModeAll:\n    for _, pool := range pools {\n        if pool.IsIncomplete {\n            return requestData, fmt.Errorf(\"...asks for all devices, but resource pool %s is currently being updated...\")\n        }\n        if pool.IsInvalid {\n            return requestData, fmt.Errorf(\"...asks for all devices, but resource pool %s is currently invalid...\")\n        }\n        // ... enumerate selectable devices from pool ...\n    }\n```\n\nThis means the `IsIncomplete` flag is the gatekeeper for `AllocationMode: All`. The old code's false-positive `IsIncomplete` for multi-node pools was the root blocker.\n\n### Scheduler Hot Path Tracing\n\n1. **PreFilter** (`dynamicresources.go:529`) \u2014 Creates the `Allocator` instance, stores it in cycle state.\n2. **Filter** (`dynamicresources.go:884`) \u2014 For each candidate node, calls `state.allocator.Allocate(ctx, node, claims)` at line 964.\n3. **`Allocate()`** (`allocator_stable.go:97`) \u2014 Calls `GatherPools()` at line 114 (the changed function), then runs the recursive backtracking allocator via `allocateOne()`.\n4. **`allocateOne()`** (`allocator_stable.go:681`) \u2014 For `AllocationMode: All`, iterates `requestData.allDevices` (line 765-778), which was populated during pool gathering.\n\n### Pool Gathering Call Chain\n\n```\nFilter() [dynamicresources.go:964]\n  -> Allocator.Allocate() [allocator_stable.go:97]\n    -> GatherPools() [pools_stable.go:58]  <-- THE CHANGED FUNCTION\n      -> nodeMatches() per slice\n      -> addSlice() per matching slice\n      -> incompletePools check (NEW: pre-filter completeness)\n    -> prepareRequest() [allocator_stable.go:364]\n      -> checks pool.IsIncomplete for AllocationMode:All\n    -> allocateOne() [allocator_stable.go:681]\n```\n\n### API Definitions for AllocationMode\n\n- **v1**: `staging/src/k8s.io/api/resource/v1/types.go:893` \u2014 `AllocationMode DeviceAllocationMode` field on `ExactDeviceRequest`\n- **v1**: `staging/src/k8s.io/api/resource/v1/types.go:1021` \u2014 `AllocationMode DeviceAllocationMode` field on `DeviceSubRequest`\n- **v1**: `staging/src/k8s.io/api/resource/v1/types.go:1112-1113` \u2014 Constants: `DeviceAllocationModeExactCount`, `DeviceAllocationModeAll`\n- **v1beta1**: `staging/src/k8s.io/api/resource/v1beta1/types.go:864`\n- **v1beta2**: `staging/src/k8s.io/api/resource/v1beta2/types.go:900`\n\n### Validation\n\n- `pkg/apis/resource/validation/validation.go:268-286` \u2014 `validateDeviceAllocationMode()`: for `All` mode, Count must be 0; for `ExactCount`, Count must be > 0.\n\n### Test Coverage\n\nNew test case added in `allocatortesting/allocator_testing.go:5093-5126`:\n- Test name: `\"allocation-mode-all-with-multi-host-resource-pool\"`\n- Creates a pool with 2 slices on different nodes (`node1`, `node2`), `ResourceSliceCount=2`\n- Claims `AllocationMode: All` from class A\n- Expects allocation to succeed on node1 with only device1 (the device from node1's slice)\n\n## Affected Components\n\n### HIGH RISK\n\n| Package | File(s) | Impact |\n|---------|---------|--------|\n| `dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/stable` | `pools_stable.go:58-149` | **Direct change site.** `GatherPools()` runs on every `Filter()` call for every node in the scheduling cycle. Extra map allocation + iteration adds overhead proportional to total ResourceSlice count. |\n| `dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/incubating` | `pools_incubating.go:58-140` | Same change, incubating allocator tier. |\n| `dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/experimental` | `pools_experimental.go:58-162` | Same change, experimental allocator tier. |\n| `scheduler/framework/plugins/dynamicresources` | `dynamicresources.go:884-1019` | **Filter() hot path.** Calls `Allocate()` which calls `GatherPools()`. Any regression here affects scheduling latency for all pods with DRA claims. Filter already has an optional timeout (`EnableDRASchedulerFilterTimeout`). |\n\n### MEDIUM RISK\n\n| Package | File(s) | Impact |\n|---------|---------|--------|\n| `dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/stable` | `allocator_stable.go:402-437` | The `AllocationMode: All` handler now sees multi-node pools as complete and enumerates devices across them. Previously unreachable code path for multi-node pools is now reachable \u2014 the `isSelectable()` and `allocateDevice()` paths will process more devices. |\n| `kubelet/cm/dra` | `manager.go:226-473` | **Kubelet PrepareResources.** The `AllocationResult` from the scheduler may now reference devices from a multi-node pool. The kubelet processes results generically (groups by driver, calls `NodePrepareResources` gRPC), so the code path is unchanged, but the _data_ is different. A device listed in the allocation result must be physically present on the node for the DRA driver to prepare it. |\n| `kubelet/cm/dra` | `claiminfo.go:57-79` | `newClaimInfoFromClaim()` parses `AllocationResult.Devices.Results` \u2014 will now see results from multi-node pool allocations. No code change needed, but more device entries per claim are possible. |\n| `pkg/apis/resource/validation` | `validation.go:268-286` | No change, but validation allows `AllocationMode: All` with Count=0. If multi-node pools produce allocations with more devices than expected, the `AllocationResultsMaxSize` check in `allocator_stable.go:758` is the only guard. |\n| `pkg/quota/v1/evaluator/core` | `resource_claims_test.go` | Quota evaluation counts devices per claim. More devices from multi-node `All` mode means higher quota consumption. |\n\n### LOW RISK\n\n| Package | File(s) | Impact |\n|---------|---------|--------|\n| `pkg/apis/resource/v1/defaults.go` | Lines 31-48 | Defaults `AllocationMode` to `ExactCount` \u2014 unaffected by this change. |\n| `pkg/apis/resource/v1beta1/conversion.go` | Lines 49-93 | API version conversion \u2014 passes `AllocationMode` through unchanged. |\n| `pkg/apis/resource/v1beta2/conversion.go` | Auto-generated | Same. |\n| `client-go applyconfigurations` | `resource/v1/devicerequest.go` etc. | Client-side builders \u2014 no behavioral change. |\n| `pkg/printers/internalversion` | `printers_test.go` | Display logic \u2014 no behavioral change. |\n| `pkg/registry/resource/resourceclaim` | `strategy.go`, `declarative_validation_test.go` | API server storage strategy \u2014 validates and stores claims, no allocation logic. |\n\n## Recommendation\n\n### Risk Mitigation Strategy\n\n1. **The `IsIncomplete` false-positive was the only thing preventing `AllocationMode: All` from working with multi-node pools.** The fix is semantically correct: completeness should be determined from the full set of slices, not the post-node-filter subset. However, the previous behavior served as an accidental safety net \u2014 it prevented allocating \"all\" devices from a pool where the scheduler only sees a subset of slices.\n\n2. **Key invariant to verify:** When `AllocationMode: All` succeeds on a node, the allocation result must only contain devices whose slices match that node. The existing code in `allocator_stable.go:419-434` iterates `pool.Slices` (which are already node-filtered by `GatherPools`), so this invariant holds \u2014 the fix does not change which slices are in a pool after node filtering, only whether the pool is marked incomplete.\n\n3. **Performance concern:** `GatherPools()` now does two passes over all slices (first to compute completeness, then to filter by node). For clusters with many ResourceSlices (e.g., 1000+ GPUs across 100 nodes), this doubles the iteration in the pool gathering phase. This runs inside the `Filter` extension point for every node candidate. Mitigation: the scheduler already has `EnableDRASchedulerFilterTimeout` and the allocator is scoped to claims for the current pod, limiting the slice set.\n\n4. **The existence of a revert commit (`a0e500ace39`)** suggests this change was previously landed and then reverted, indicating prior issues were encountered. The current HEAD has the change re-applied. The revert/re-apply history warrants extra scrutiny.\n\n### Testing Plan\n\n1. **Unit tests (existing + new):**\n   - New test `\"allocation-mode-all-with-multi-host-resource-pool\"` in `allocatortesting/allocator_testing.go:5093` covers the core scenario.\n   - Existing tests for `AllocationMode: All` in single-node scenarios remain in `allocator_testing.go` (search for `DeviceAllocationModeAll`).\n   - Run: `go test ./staging/src/k8s.io/dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/...`\n\n2. **Integration tests:**\n   - `test/integration/dra/dra_test.go:223` \u2014 `TestDRA` covers end-to-end DRA scheduling.\n   - `test/integration/scheduler_perf/dra/dra_test.go:41` \u2014 Performance benchmarks.\n   - Run: `go test ./test/integration/dra/...`\n\n3. **E2E tests:**\n   - `test/e2e/dra/dra.go` \u2014 Extensive allocation tests including multi-node scenarios (\"must allow multiple allocations and consume capacity\" at line 1899).\n\n4. **Recommended additional tests:**\n   - **Multi-node pool with incomplete slices + `AllocationMode: All`:** Verify the scheduler correctly blocks allocation when a multi-node pool is genuinely incomplete (generation mismatch or slice count mismatch).\n   - **Multi-node pool with `AllocationMode: All` and device selectors:** Ensure CEL selector evaluation works correctly when the pool spans nodes but only node-local devices are enumerated.\n   - **Quota impact test:** Verify that `AllocationMode: All` from a multi-node pool with N devices on the local node correctly reports N device allocations for quota purposes (not the total across all nodes).\n   - **Scale test:** Benchmark `GatherPools()` with 500+ ResourceSlices across 50+ pools to measure the overhead of the double-pass iteration.\n   - **Concurrent scheduling test:** Two pods requesting `AllocationMode: All` from the same multi-node pool should not double-allocate devices \u2014 the `deviceInUse()` check at `allocator_stable.go:1205` and `allocatedDevices` tracking should prevent this, but it needs validation with multi-node pools specifically.\n\n5. **Risk of regression if the change has bugs:**\n   - **False-negative `IsIncomplete`:** If the pre-filter completeness check has a bug (e.g., slice grouping by wrong key), a genuinely incomplete pool could be marked complete, leading `AllocationMode: All` to allocate a partial set of devices. The allocation would succeed but miss devices still being registered.\n   - **Scheduler crash/panic:** If `slices[0]` is accessed on an empty slice group in the completeness check (line 75 in the new code: `generation := slices[0].Spec.Pool.Generation`), this would panic. This is guarded by the map construction which only creates entries when slices exist, but deserves a defensive check.\n   - **Kubelet failure:** If the allocation result includes a device not physically available on the node, the DRA driver's `NodePrepareResources` gRPC call will fail, causing the pod to enter `ContainerCreating` state indefinitely. This would be the most user-visible failure mode.\n   - **Performance degradation at scale:** The extra map allocation and iteration in `GatherPools()` could measurably increase scheduling latency in clusters with thousands of ResourceSlices, since this runs in the Filter hot path for every candidate node.\n",

The old code's false-positive `IsIncomplete` for multi-node pools was the root blocker.\n\n### Scheduler Hot Path Tracing\n\n1. **PreFilter** (`dynamicresources.go:529`) \u2014 Creates the `Allocator` instance, stores it in cycle state.\n2. **Filter** (`dynamicresources.go:884`) \u2014 For each candidate node, calls `state.allocator.Allocate(ctx, node, claims)` at line 964.\n3. **`Allocate()`** (`allocator_stable.go:97`) \u2014 Calls `GatherPools()` at line 114 (the changed function), then runs the recursive backtracking allocator via `allocateOne()`.\n4. **`allocateOne()`** (`allocator_stable.go:681`) \u2014 For `AllocationMode: All`, iterates `requestData.allDevices` (line 765-778), which was populated during pool gathering.\n\n### Pool Gathering Call Chain\n\n```\nFilter() [dynamicresources.go:964]\n  -> Allocator.Allocate() [allocator_stable.go:97]\n    -> GatherPools() [pools_stable.go:58]  <-- THE CHANGED FUNCTION\n      -> nodeMatches() per slice\n      -> addSlice() per matching slice\n      -> incompletePools check (NEW: pre-filter completeness)\n    -> prepareRequest() [allocator_stable.go:364]\n      -> checks pool.IsIncomplete for AllocationMode:All\n    -> allocateOne() [allocator_stable.go:681]\n```\n\n### API Definitions for AllocationMode\n\n- **v1**: `staging/src/k8s.io/api/resource/v1/types.go:893` \u2014 `AllocationMode DeviceAllocationMode` field on `ExactDeviceRequest`\n- **v1**: `staging/src/k8s.io/api/resource/v1/types.go:1021` \u2014 `AllocationMode DeviceAllocationMode` field on `DeviceSubRequest`\n- **v1**: `staging/src/k8s.io/api/resource/v1/types.go:1112-1113` \u2014 Constants: `DeviceAllocationModeExactCount`, `DeviceAllocationModeAll`\n- **v1beta1**: `staging/src/k8s.io/api/resource/v1beta1/types.go:864`\n- **v1beta2**: `staging/src/k8s.io/api/resource/v1beta2/types.go:900`\n\n### Validation\n\n- `pkg/apis/resource/validation/validation.go:268-286` \u2014 `validateDeviceAllocationMode()`: for `All` mode, Count must be 0; for `ExactCount`, Count must be > 0.\n\n### Test Coverage\n\nNew test case added in `allocatortesting/allocator_testing.go:5093-5126`:\n- Test name: `\"allocation-mode-all-with-multi-host-resource-pool\"`\n- Creates a pool with 2 slices on different nodes (`node1`, `node2`), `ResourceSliceCount=2`\n- Claims `AllocationMode: All` from class A\n- Expects allocation to succeed on node1 with only device1 (the device from node1's slice)\n\n## Affected Components\n\n### HIGH RISK\n\n| Package | File(s) | Impact |\n|---------|---------|--------|\n| `dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/stable` | `pools_stable.go:58-149` | **Direct change site.** `GatherPools()` runs on every `Filter()` call for every node in the scheduling cycle. Extra map allocation + iteration adds overhead proportional to total ResourceSlice count. |\n| `dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/incubating` | `pools_incubating.go:58-140` | Same change, incubating allocator tier. |\n| `dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/experimental` | `pools_experimental.go:58-162` | Same change, experimental allocator tier. |\n| `scheduler/framework/plugins/dynamicresources` | `dynamicresources.go:884-1019` | **Filter() hot path.** Calls `Allocate()` which calls `GatherPools()`. Any regression here affects scheduling latency for all pods with DRA claims. Filter already has an optional timeout (`EnableDRASchedulerFilterTimeout`). |\n\n### MEDIUM RISK\n\n| Package | File(s) | Impact |\n|---------|---------|--------|\n| `dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/internal/stable` | `allocator_stable.go:402-437` | The `AllocationMode: All` handler now sees multi-node pools as complete and enumerates devices across them. Previously unreachable code path for multi-node pools is now reachable \u2014 the `isSelectable()` and `allocateDevice()` paths will process more devices. |\n| `kubelet/cm/dra` | `manager.go:226-473` | **Kubelet PrepareResources.** The `AllocationResult` from the scheduler may now reference devices from a multi-node pool. The kubelet processes results generically (groups by driver, calls `NodePrepareResources` gRPC), so the code path is unchanged, but the _data_ is different. A device listed in the allocation result must be physically present on the node for the DRA driver to prepare it. |\n| `kubelet/cm/dra` | `claiminfo.go:57-79` | `newClaimInfoFromClaim()` parses `AllocationResult.Devices.Results` \u2014 will now see results from multi-node pool allocations. No code change needed, but more device entries per claim are possible. |\n| `pkg/apis/resource/validation` | `validation.go:268-286` | No change, but validation allows `AllocationMode: All` with Count=0. If multi-node pools produce allocations with more devices than expected, the `AllocationResultsMaxSize` check in `allocator_stable.go:758` is the only guard. |\n| `pkg/quota/v1/evaluator/core` | `resource_claims_test.go` | Quota evaluation counts devices per claim. More devices from multi-node `All` mode means higher quota consumption. |\n\n### LOW RISK\n\n| Package | File(s) | Impact |\n|---------|---------|--------|\n| `pkg/apis/resource/v1/defaults.go` | Lines 31-48 | Defaults `AllocationMode` to `ExactCount` \u2014 unaffected by this change. |\n| `pkg/apis/resource/v1beta1/conversion.go` | Lines 49-93 | API version conversion \u2014 passes `AllocationMode` through unchanged. |\n| `pkg/apis/resource/v1beta2/conversion.go` | Auto-generated | Same. |\n| `client-go applyconfigurations` | `resource/v1/devicerequest.go` etc. | Client-side builders \u2014 no behavioral change. |\n| `pkg/printers/internalversion` | `printers_test.go` | Display logic \u2014 no behavioral change. |\n| `pkg/registry/resource/resourceclaim` | `strategy.go`, `declarative_validation_test.go` | API server storage strategy \u2014 validates and stores claims, no allocation logic. |\n\n## Recommendation\n\n### Risk Mitigation Strategy\n\n1. **The `IsIncomplete` false-positive was the only thing preventing `AllocationMode: All` from working with multi-node pools.** The fix is semantically correct: completeness should be determined from the full set of slices, not the post-node-filter subset. However, the previous behavior served as an accidental safety net \u2014 it prevented allocating \"all\" devices from a pool where the scheduler only sees a subset of slices.\n\n2. **Key invariant to verify:** When `AllocationMode: All` succeeds on a node, the allocation result must only contain devices whose slices match that node. The existing code in `allocator_stable.go:419-434` iterates `pool.Slices` (which are already node-filtered by `GatherPools`), so this invariant holds \u2014 the fix does not change which slices are in a pool after node filtering, only whether the pool is marked incomplete.\n\n3. **Performance concern:** `GatherPools()` now does two passes over all slices (first to compute completeness, then to filter by node). For clusters with many ResourceSlices (e.g., 1000+ GPUs across 100 nodes), this doubles the iteration in the pool gathering phase. This runs inside the `Filter` extension point for every node candidate. Mitigation: the scheduler already has `EnableDRASchedulerFilterTimeout` and the allocator is scoped to claims for the current pod, limiting the slice set.\n\n4. **The existence of a revert commit (`a0e500ace39`)** suggests this change was previously landed and then reverted, indicating prior issues were encountered. The current HEAD has the change re-applied. The revert/re-apply history warrants extra scrutiny.\n\n### Testing Plan\n\n1. **Unit tests (existing + new):**\n   - New test `\"allocation-mode-all-with-multi-host-resource-pool\"` in `allocatortesting/allocator_testing.go:5093` covers the core scenario.\n   - Existing tests for `AllocationMode: All` in single-node scenarios remain in `allocator_testing.go` (search for `DeviceAllocationModeAll`).\n   - Run: `go test ./staging/src/k8s.io/dynamic-resource-allocation/structured/...`\n\n2. **Integration tests:**\n   - `test/integration/dra/dra_test.go:223` \u2014 `TestDRA` covers end-to-end DRA scheduling.\n   - `test/integration/scheduler_perf/dra/dra_test.go:41` \u2014 Performance benchmarks.\n   - Run: `go test ./test/integration/dra/...`\n\n3. **E2E tests:**\n   - `test/e2e/dra/dra.go` \u2014 Extensive allocation tests including multi-node scenarios (\"must allow multiple allocations and consume capacity\" at line 1899).\n\n4. **Recommended additional tests:**\n   - **Multi-node pool with incomplete slices + `AllocationMode: All`:** Verify the scheduler correctly blocks allocation when a multi-node pool is genuinely incomplete (generation mismatch or slice count mismatch).\n   - **Multi-node pool with `AllocationMode: All` and device selectors:** Ensure CEL selector evaluation works correctly when the pool spans nodes but only node-local devices are enumerated.\n   - **Quota impact test:** Verify that `AllocationMode: All` from a multi-node pool with N devices on the local node correctly reports N device allocations for quota purposes (not the total across all nodes).\n   - **Scale test:** Benchmark `GatherPools()` with 500+ ResourceSlices across 50+ pools to measure the overhead of the double-pass iteration.\n   - **Concurrent scheduling test:** Two pods requesting `AllocationMode: All` from the same multi-node pool should not double-allocate devices \u2014 the `deviceInUse()` check at `allocator_stable.go:1205` and `allocatedDevices` tracking should prevent this, but it needs validation with multi-node pools specifically.\n\n5. **Risk of regression if the change has bugs:**\n   - **False-negative `IsIncomplete`:** If the pre-filter completeness check has a bug (e.g., slice grouping by wrong key), a genuinely incomplete pool could be marked complete, leading `AllocationMode: All` to allocate a partial set of devices. The allocation would succeed but miss devices still being registered.\n   - **Scheduler crash/panic:** If `slices[0]` is accessed on an empty slice group in the completeness check (line 75 in the new code: `generation := slices[0].Spec.Pool.Generation`), this would panic. This is guarded by the map construction which only creates entries when slices exist, but deserves a defensive check.\n   - **Kubelet failure:** If the allocation result includes a device not physically available on the node, the DRA driver's `NodePrepareResources` gRPC call will fail, causing the pod to enter `ContainerCreating` state indefinitely. This would be the most user-visible failure mode.\n   - **Performance degradation at scale:** The extra map allocation and iteration in `GatherPools()` could measurably increase scheduling latency in clusters with thousands of ResourceSlices, since this runs in the Filter hot path for every candidate node.\n",

1. WRITE /logs/agent/investigation.md
# Investigation Report

## Summary

The change (commit `2e534d6da10`) modifies `GatherPools()` in all three allocator tiers (stable, incubating, experimental) to compute pool completeness _before_ filtering slices by node affinity, which allows `AllocationMode: All` to succeed for multi-node resource pools where only a subset of the pool's slices target the scheduling node. Previously, such pools were incorrectly marked as incomplete (because the per-node slice count did not match `ResourceSliceCount`), causing allocation to fail with "pool is currently being updated."

## Root Cause

The scope of the change is narrow in terms of files touched (4 files, `pools_{stable,incubating,experimental}.go` + test), but the behavioral impact is broad: any workload using `AllocationMode: All` with resource pools whose slices span multiple nodes will now successfully allocate, whereas before it was silently blocked. The core bug was in the `IsIncomplete` computation inside `GatherPools()` — it compared `len(pool.Slices)` (post-node-filter) against `pool.Slices[0].Spec.Pool.ResourceSliceCount` (the total across all nodes), which always mismatch for multi-node pools. The fix introduces a pre-filter completeness check using the full set of slices grouped by pool identifier.

### Components affected:
1. **Structured allocator pool gathering** — the `GatherPools()` function is the direct change site.
2. **Scheduler DRA plugin Filter path** — `GatherPools()` is called from `Allocator.Allocate()` which is invoked during the `Filter` extension point, the scheduler's hot path evaluated for every node.
3. **Downstream kubelet/device-plugin behavior** — the kubelet sees different `AllocationResult` contents (potentially more devices from a single pool), but the kubelet code itself is not chang
... (truncated)
